 jab aap lagaataar vah kaam karte hai, jinhen karne ke liye aapkaa man nahin maanata yaa aap khush nahin hai, to chaahe aapke paas kitne hi dost kyon na hon, ant main aap khud ko akelaa hi paaenge depressant ke saath
 So it is important that you identify who is really your friend and from whom you know only your life
 
 
 tippaniyan Expectations don't dominate depressant kii ek or badi vajah he apekshaayen
 
 
 Yes, people have certain expectations from us and the same amount or more from us
 jab ye apekshaayen puri nahin ho paati, to maansik ashaanti or antardvand janm detaa he depressant ko
 Many times the family expects a lot from the children and pressures them, sometimes the children pressurize their family to fulfill their expectations
 to behatar he ki aap na hi dusron se apeksha karen or na hi unki apekshaaon ko khud par haaavee hone den
 First of all, it is important to know that it is not right to name every problem as depression
 hamane khud ko inta samvedansheel or aviveki bana liya he ki jivan main aane vaale utaar-chadhaav ko jhel nahin pate
 Instead of accepting the struggles and challenges of life, we start running away from them
 chunautiyon se bhaagane se ye or vikaraal rup le leti hai or ant main jab ham inase deal nahin kar pate to jo dabaav ham mahasoos karte hai use depressant kaa naam de dete hai
 this is not right
 jivan main aane vaali chunautiyon ko sweekaar kar unase laden na ki unhen depressant kaa naam den
 Believe Therapy depressant main jane kii ek badi vajah he, khud se bilive kam hona
 Most people find themselves lacking, and it has become a habit of everyone
 koi khud se khush nahin
 Some do not like their nose, some face pimples, some increase their weight, and some feel that the relationship is not going well because of it
 
 
 khud main bahut-si kamiyaan talash kar ham khud se nafrat karnaa shuru kar dete hai
 We believe that 'we are not good'
 ’ yahi yakeen depressant kii neenv hota he
 So start loving yourself from today
 yakeen karen ki aap behad khubsurat hai, khud ko roj shishe main dekhen
 Look at yourself and say that you are very good, i love you
 
 
 har dost dost nahin hota In today's time, the thing that the youth feel the most pressure is peer pressure
 ji haa, aksar ham apane saath padhane vaale group, kuch saal se saath rahe doston ko hi apana sachcha hitaishi maan baithte hai
 Keeping ourselves right in their eyes, following their advice and doing many things that we do not want to do at all, but in the name of pressure and friendship of those so-called friends
 aise kaamon kaa ant hota he depressant par
 
 
 When you constantly do things that you don't mind doing or you are not happy, no matter how many friends you have, in the end you will find yourself alone with depression
 isliye yah jaruri he ki aap is baat kii sahi pahchaan karen ki koun asal main aapkaa dost he or kisase aapaki mahaj jaan pahchaan
 
 
 The comments apekshaayen haaavee na hon Expectations are another major cause of depression
 
 
 ji haa, kuch apekshaayen logon ko hamase hoti hai or usee maatra main yaa usase adhik hamen logon se
 When these expectations are not fulfilled, mental disturbance and internal depression give rise to depression
 kai baar parivaar vaale bacchon se behad apeksha karte hai or un par dabaav banaate hai, to kai baar bachche apane parijanon se unki apekshaayen puri karne kaa dabaav banaate hai
 So it is better that you neither expect from others nor let their expectations dominate you
 bilive therapy One of the main reasons for going into depression, is a low self-confidence
 zyaadaatar log khud main kamiyaan hi talashte hai or yah sabaki aadat si ho gai he
 Nobody is happy with themselves
 kisi ko apni naak pasand nahin, kisi ko chehre ke muhaanse, kisi ko apana badha vajan, to kisi ko lagata he ki relationships uski vajah se thik nahin chal rahaa
 
 
 We start hating ourselves by finding many shortcomings in ourselves
 ham yakeen kar lete hai ki ‘ham achche nahin
 'this belief is the foundation of depression
 isliye aaj se hi khud se pyaar karnaa shuru karen
 Make sure you are very beautiful, see yourself in the mirror everyday
 khud se nazren mila kar kahen ki tum bahut achche ho, main tumhen pyaar karti hum
